 ' Know about the highways of the world where sweet music is produced from the roads when cars are moving
 jo logon ke safar ko yaadgaar banaata he:1
 The Asphaltophone: Where: Jiling, Denmark What is special: The technique of producing music on the highway was discovered in 1995
 denmark ke do kalakaar footpath marker takanic ke saath aae or unhone haive par bots-dots jaisi rumbal strip taiyaar kii
 a sweet melody is heard as the car passes over these markings
 2
 Musical Highway, Route 66 Where: New Mexicokya Hai Special: Special rumble strips exist on old Route 66 between Albuquerque and Tigeras
 jab gaadiyaan 45 mile prati ghante kii raftaar (bilkul 45 mile) se un par guzarati hai, to unase ek sangeet nikalataa he
 The musical highway makes this beauty even more spectacular
 3
 Subaru Highway: Japan: What is special: An accident happened with Shinjua Shinoda in Japan
 kaam ke dauraan galati se buldozer ne sadak ko kharonch diya
 When carts came out of that road, sweet and interesting music was produced
 isko doharaakar japan ne shinjua ke netritv main 4 musical road banaae
 These are present in Hokkaido, Wakayama, Shinjuoka and Gunma
 4
 Civic Musical Road: Where: Lancaster, California What is special: The musical stretch in Lancaster is like a second stretch
 isko pehle ek rihaishi ilaake main lagaaya gaya tha lekin usase paidaa hone vaali awaazon se tang aakar kuch hi hafton main vahaan ke logon ne shikaayat kar di

 5
 Singing Road: Nanyang, South Korea What is special: The stretch here is designed to sound like the nursery rhyme 'mary had a little lamb' when the train passed over it

 Here we will tell about some important facts related to Hindi language, about which you are hardly aware
 
 
 1
 The Hindi language is also spoken in Mauritius, Fiji, Suriname, Trinidad and Tobago
 2
 Hindi is one of the many languages that can be used to create a web address
 3
 The Hindi word is derived from the Persian word 'hind'
 iskaa matlab sindhu nadi ke kshetra se he
 4
 samvidhan sabha ne hindi bhashaa ko aadhikarik bhashaa ke rup main 14 sitambar 1949 ko chunaa tha
 For this reason, 14 September is celebrated every year as Hindi Day
 5
 In 1981, Bihar replaced Hindi language with offices in Urdu language
 isi ke saath bihar hindi ko apnaane vaala desh kaa pehla rajya ban gaya
 6
 1965 main hindi ko bharat kiadhikarik bhashaake rup main sweekaar kar liya gaya
 7
 lagbhag 500 million log hindi bhashaa kaa prayog karte hai
 8
 1805 main chhapi lallu laal kii kitaab 'prem sagar' ko hindi kii pehali kitaab mana jaataa he
 This book describes the pastimes of Lord Krishna
 9

 Police have arrested three suspected terrorists in Amritsar, Punjab
 jinase police ko ek aatanki modul ke bare main pataa chalaa he
 These suspected terrorists were on the instructions of their masters in Pakistan, Belgium and Britain to carry out anti-national activities
 police mahanireekshak (counter intelligence) em
 F
 faarki ne bataaya ki punjab police kii counter intelligence ikai ne ekatankimodul kaa pataa lagaaya he
 In which terrorists sitting abroad have been recruited by provoking some people from the state to carry out anti-national activities
 gopneey soochna ke aadhaar par karrwai karte hue police ne gurpal singh, major singh or rachpal singh ko alag alag sthanon se giraftaar kiya he
 Police also recovered two 9 mm and 30 bore pistols, magazines and 16 cartridges from them
 aiji faarki ne daawa kiya ki ye aaropee belgium, britain or pakistan main kuch vaanchit aatankiyon ke sampark main the
 All three were tasked to restore terrorism in Punjab
 faarki ke mutabik ye vaanchit aatanki jagadish singh urf bhura (belgium), kuldeep singh urf keepa siddhu, jasbir singh urf jassi (britain) or ranjit singh urf nita pakistan or khalistaan jindabad bal ke liye kaam kar rahe the
 All three terrorists are being interrogated
 bihar main rashtriya janata dal or bhartiya janata party main mitti prakaran par aarope-pratyarope kaa khel jari he
 While another Rashtriya Janata Dal leader is claiming that the Chief Secretary has given a clean chit after being satisfied with the report of the forest department on this issue, the officials of the state forest department are saying something else
 adhikariyon kaa kahana he ki clin chit to dur rajya ke mukhya sachiv anjani kumaar singh ne vibhaag ko is baat kii jaanch karaane ke liye kaha he ki patna ke sanjay gandhi jaivik udyaan main jo nau lakh kii mitti ai uskaa strot kya he? saath hi udyaan main mitti kii itani oonchi sadak kaa auchity kya he? However, till now Rashtriya Janata Dal's medicine was that all works in the organic park have been found correct after an investigation by the Chief Secretary
 lekin is maamle main rajya ke van vibhaag kaa kahana he ki na to abhi tak koi jaanch kaa aadesh hua he or na hi kisi ko bedaag mana gaya he
 Meanwhile, the Rashtriya Janata Dal held a press conference on Monday with its senior leader and former MP Jagadanand Singh
 isamen singh, jo rajya ke purv van mantri rah chuke hai, ne susheel modi par hamalaa bolaa
 Giving papers, Jagdanand Singh claimed that the forest department of the state does not work on the basis of tender
 singh ne yahaan tak kaha ki jab modi nitish sarkaar main mantri the tab 628 kaa kaam hua lekin uske liye kabhi tender nahin nikaale gaye
 Jagadanand also dragged Nitish Kumar in this case and said that if the work of 90 lakhs without tender is considered invalid, then the question of expenditure of Rs 631 crore without tender in the second term of NDA will also be raised
 tippaniyan However, when asked about Jagdanand's correspondent conference on Monday evening, BJP leader Sushil Modi said that he no longer wants to give much importance to the soil case because now the entire controversy is focused on how Lalu Yadav in the last few years How he named his benami property to the people of his family
 or jahaan tak clin chit dene kaa prashn he, vah van vibhaag ke adhikariyon ne lalu yadav ko bachaane ke liye unke mutabik taiyaar kiya
 However, Modi has written a letter to the Central Zoo Authority requesting to send an investigation team to the Sanjay Gandhi Biological Park in Patna
 darasal is puure vivaad kii jad main he patna ke beli road par lalu yadav ke parivaar ke logon ke swaamitv vaali jameen par ek maal kaa nirmaan
 Modi alleged that the soil that was found for the underground parking of this mall was sold at Sanjay Gandhi Biological Park in Patna and worked for it in violation of the rules at night
 baad main van vibhaag ne safai di ki yah kaam 90 lakh kaa nahin balki maatr 40 lakh kaa tha
 Lalu Yadav's eldest son Tej Pratap Yadav is currently the state's forest minister and he has not said anything about the entire controversy so far
 haalanki abhi tak rashtriya janata dal kaa dawa tha ki jaivik udyaan main saare kaam mukhya sachiv ne ek jaanch ke baad sahi paae hai
 But in this case, the State Forest Department says that no investigation has been ordered nor any has been considered untainted
 is bich rashtriya janata dal ne somvaar ko apane varisht netaa or purv saansad jagadanand singh se ek samvaadadaata sammelan karavaaya
 In this, Singh, who has been the former forest minister of the state, attacked Sushil Modi
 jagadanand singh ne kagajaat dete hue daawa kiya ki rajya ke van vibhaag main tender ke aadhaar par kaary nahin hota he
 Singh even said that when Modi was a minister in the Nitish government, the work of 628 was done but tenders were never withdrawn for that
 jagadanand ne nitish kumaar ko bhi is prakaran main ghasitate hue kaha ki agar bina tender ke 90 lakh ke kaary ko avaidh maan liya jaae to phir rajg ke duusare kaarykaal main bina tender ke 631 karod ke kharche par bhi prashn khadaa ho jayega
 The comments haalanki somvaar kii shaam jagadanand ke samvaadadaata sammelan ke bare main puche jane par bijepi netaa susheel modi kaa kahana tha ki ve ab mitti prakaran ko bahut zyada mahatv nahin dena chaahate kyonki ab yah puraa vivaad is baat par kendrit he ki pichley kuch varshon main lalu yadav ne apni benami sampatti kaise apane parivaar ke logon ke naam kii
 And as far as giving clean chit is concerned, he was prepared by the forest department officials to save Lalu Yadav according to him
 haalanki modi ne kendriya zu athurity ko ek patr likhakar patna ke sanjay gandhi jaivik udyaan main ek jaanch dal bhejne kaa aagrah kiya he
 Actually, at the root of this whole controversy is the construction of a consignment on the land owned by the people of Lalu Yadav's family on Bailey Road in Patna
 modi ne aarope lagaaya tha ki is mal kii underground parking ke liye jo mitti nikali gai vah patna ke sanjay gandhi jaivik udyaan main bechi gai or iske liye raat main niyamon kaa ulanghan kar kaam kiya jaataa tha

 Famous filmmaker director Yash Chopra, who has said goodbye to the world, has created a new definition of romance through several films in his five-decade Bollywood career
 chopra ne bhartiya cinema kii sabase saphaltam filmon kaa nirdesan kiya
 From 'angry Young Man' Amitabh Bachchan's 'wall' to 'badshah' Shah Rukh Khan's 'dil To Pagal Hai', Yash Chopra went behind the camera and held the pulse of the audience for decades
 chopra or bachchan kii jodi ne bollywood kii ‚Äòkabhi kabhi‚Äô or ‚Äòtrishul‚Äô jaisi filmein bhi deen
 If Shah Rukh Khan is the king of films then Yash Chopra is the 'kingmaker'
 unhone hi apane camere kii kalakaari se kai abhinaytaon ko bollywood kaa superstar bana diya
 Although he started his career by making different types of films, he will always be remembered for films like 'chandni', 'dilwale Dulhania Le Jayenge', 'silsila'
 unki style kii romantic filmon ke liye ‚Äòyash chopra romance‚Äô lafj ijad hua
 He made more than 50 films in his five-decade career
 yash chopra ko unke filmi kariyar main chah rashtriya film puraskaar or 11 filmphere puraskaron se nawaja gaya
 He received the Filmfare Award for Best Director four times for his films
 lahore main 27 sitambar 1932 ko janme chopra bantwaare ke baad bharat aa gaye
 He wanted to become an engineer
 haalanki filmanirmaan ke liye apane jazbe ke chalate vah mumbai chale gaye, jahaan unhone aies johar or phir apane nirmaataa nirdeshak bhai biaar chopra ke saath sahaayak nirdeshak ban gaye
 After the success of films, the Chopra brothers made many films in the 50s and 60s
